when they repented with sorrow, and said that they had gone
astray,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
said, “Certainly if our Lady of Light did not have mercy upon us,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then
we might have become one of those that perish from the earth but do not
enter paradise forever.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">        </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.150 And
when Miriam and Moses returned to their people, full of worry and
concern,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
prophetess said, “What you have done makes absolutely no sense,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you were
told you have a loving and kind Goddess that cares for you.” </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And as
she took away the tablets, they fell and
broke,<a href="#_ftn93" id="_ftnref93"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[93]</span></span></span></span></a> and
she said,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“It does
not matter; you are not ready for these and we have more learning for
you.” </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And the
prophetess took Alana and lovingly caressed her hair and head and said,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Because
you are the daughter of my mother also, I forgive you. I know that this
seems different, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but I do
not see it in such a manner, I am not worried if my enemies should
rejoice in my pain, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
I am not one of the wicked people. You all have many things to
learn.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.151
Miriam said, “O Lady of Light, forgive my sister and my people, and
receive us into your great mercy;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For
those that exercise mercy freely, are the most merciful
themselves.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.152
Certainly as for those people who took a molten calf as a goddess, they
were led astray, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet
Goddess still loves them and will continue to show them the way to
peace, love and happiness </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">though
Her, and this is the reward of those that have false imaginings
regarding Goddess.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                              </span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.153 But
to those people that have made mistakes, and afterwards repent,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
believe in Goddess, certainly the Lady of Light thereafter</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">will
be merciful and kind to them in an exceedingly gracious manner.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.154 And
when the disappointment of Miriam was appeased, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">she had
Moses carry the tablet away for her; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
what was written on them was a direction and mercy for those that
greatly loved Goddess.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                    
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.155 And
Miriam chose out of her people seventy women to go up to the
mountain</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">with her
at an appointed time, when a storm of lightening and thunder took them
away, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but she
said, “O Lady of Light, if you desired you could have taken them away
before, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and also
me, but why destroy us for the things that only foolish people have
done? </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For we
know that this lifetime is only a trial, and those with good hearts are
easily directed by You, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and You
direct them often. For you are our great Protectress, therefore forgive
us,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">be
merciful to us, for you are the most generous of those that
forgive.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.156
“And please write down for us all the good we have done in this
world,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and in
the life to come, for we desire to be directed by You.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
answered, “I do not punish in the sense that you understand this,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">I do not
have negative human emotions, my mercy extends over all things,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and these
women did not die, except it was their appointed time,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and none
asked for an extension, so please understand , </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for I
will record the good deeds for those that love me,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
give alms to the poor, and those that believe in the signs and miracles
sent from Me and heaven;<span style="mso-tab-count:1">           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.157 and
those that follow the prophetesses, even those that are
illiterate,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
shall find recorded in the law and the gospel complete peace and love;
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
will command what is just, and will forbid them which is evil; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and will
allow them the good things which may have been forbidden before, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and will
prohibit those things which are bad; and she will ease them of a heavy
religious burden, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and of
the yokes which were once upon them.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And those
that believe in her work and honor her, assist her and follow the light,
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which
has been sent down to her, shall be happy.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.158
Tell the people, “O women, certainly I am the messenger of Goddess sent
to you all; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">to Her
belongs the Queendom of heaven and earth, for there is no Goddess but
She;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She gives
life and She directs the end of your life, and She will be with you when
you die,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Believe
then in Goddess and her apostles, ascended mistresses and
prophetesses,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even the
illiterate ones, who believe in Goddess and Her Word;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
follow Her, that you might be rightfully directed.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                      
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.159 Of
the people of Miriam there were some women that directed the others with
the truth, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
they acted justly according to the same.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                      
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.160 And
the Jews were divided into twelve tribes, as if they were so many
nations.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
heaven spoke its revelations to a prophetess, when the women asked where
they might find water,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
people were told, “Strike this rock with the rod of the
prophetess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and from
there gushed twelve fountains, and women knew where to find water for
their families.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
heaven caused clouds to overshadow them, and manna and quails to descend
to them saying,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Eat of
the good things which we have given you for food,”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but some
of them did not, and those people did not injure any entity in heaven,
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet
they injured their own souls.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                        
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.161 And
some of them were able to remember the time when it was said to
them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Live in
this city and eat of the provision found therein if you will,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and say
‘forgiveness’ and enter the gate worshiping;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then
you sins will be pardoned and the believers will be given more.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.162 But
those people who were not believers among them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">changed
the expression into another which had not been given to them, and made
it a joke,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and it
made the people living there anxious and uneasy,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">instead
of spreading love and peace, which is what Goddess intended.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Because
of this, they were sent more teachers and prophetesses from heaven,
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
they might learn properly, because they regressed.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.163 And
we have asked them concerning the city, which was situated on the sea,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when the
fish came near them on the Sabbath; they appeared plentifully near the
sea, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but every
other day of the week they did not come; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this
was a test for those that were strong and righteous.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                    
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.164 And
when some of the women said to the others,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Why do
you warn a people whom Goddess will destroy, or will punish with a
grievous punishment?” </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The
believers answered, “You do not understand, Goddess does not destroy,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor does
She punish in a way that you understand, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">there
are plans for even the wicked doers, and you need not question
Her.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                   
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.165 But
when they had forgotten the warnings which had been given them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
heaven saved those that preached against others doing evil,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and we
inflicted upon the evil doers plans so that they could learn themselves
not to do evil, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
we had noticed their wickedness.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.166 And
when some proudly refused to desist from what had been forbidden
them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">some were
transformed into apes by the demons, who then blamed this on Goddess,
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
they were banned from their village for a period of time.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.167 And
remember when your Lady of Light declared that She would send against
the Jews, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">until the
day of resurrection, a nation that would afflict them with a grievous
oppression,<a href="#_ftn94" id="_ftnref94"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[94]</span></span></span></span></a>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">know that
there is conflict in this world that does not exist in heaven, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
that your Lady of Light is swift to love, and also ready to forgive, and
She is exceedingly merciful.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">         
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.168
Heaven has dispersed rulers among the nations in the earth.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some of
them are upright persons, and some of them are otherwise.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
heaven also provided them with prosperity and adversity, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so
that they might refrain from being disobedient.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.169 And
many descendants have come from them, women that have inherited the Book
of Law, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this
Korana, who receive the temporal bribes of this
world,<a href="#_ftn95" id="_ftnref95"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[95]</span></span></span></span></a> they
say, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“This is
not the covenant of the Book of Law, this Korana, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and all
our sins will be forgiven of us, no matter what we do,” </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and if a
temporary advantage like this is told to them to them by anyone, they
readily accept it. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But this
Good Book has given to them, and so they should not should speak of
Goddess in such a manner, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
people can do evil over and over again, and still they say She will
forgive them </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">without
Her guidance, and repentance; this is only a vain imagining, but it is
not the truth. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Yet they
diligently read what been written therein.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But the
enjoyment of the next life is best for those that love Goddess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
love to follow Her directions, than the wicked gains of such people. You
should understand this.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">            </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.170 And
for those who hold fast to the Book of the Law, this Korana, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
are regular in prayer, the reward of the righteous shall never
perish.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.171 And
when heaven shook the mountain of Sinai over the
people,<a href="#_ftn96" id="_ftnref96"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[96]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
people were told to follow the Scripture to guard against evil.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.172 And
when Goddess drew forth their posterity from the abdomens of Eve and
Adam, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and asked
them, “Am I not your beloved Lady of Light?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">They
answered, “Yes, you are and shall be our beloved Lady of Light,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
of understanding, wisdom, mercy and love.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She
kissed each, and they all return to Eve and Adam. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This was
done unless you say at the day of resurrection,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Assuredly,
we did not know or understand this matter because we were never
told.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                                    
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.173 Or
perhaps you might say, “Certainly our ancestors worshiped</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
earthly idols of power, greed, self absorption, and so did we,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
we are their posterity that succeeded them,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
will you destroy us for what vain people have done before us?”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.174 In
such a manner, we explain our signs and miracles,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so
that people might refrain from holding onto their vanities.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.175 And
remember how the Jews, in their herstory, recall a certain
prophetess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
heaven departed from her company because she was followed by Evil and
seduced by
it.<a href="#_ftn97" id="_ftnref97"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[97]</span></span></span></span></a>
<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                     </span><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes"> </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.176 But
had she desired, she could have been led by heaven to teach new
wisdom;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but she
inclined to those dark entities of the earth, and followed her dark
desires.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">As a
result, her likeness is as the likeness of a dog with a long tongue,
which,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">if you
drive her away, she sticks out her long tongue, or if you leave her
alone,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">she will
also stick out her long tongue. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This is
the likeness of the people who accuse believers </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">of having
false signs and miracles when they do not.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">When
they say such things, remind them of this herstory, so that they might
reconsider.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                  </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.177 For
evil is the life of people who accuse heaven’s signs and miracles of
being false,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when
they are not, and thereby they injure their own soul.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.178
Whomever wants Goddess to direct her, she will be rightly
directed;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
whomever decides to follow the dark entities, it shall be as if their
life never existed, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
only love survives; hate and evil do not.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                      
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.179
Moreover, heaven has created on earth a life of hell for many of the
genii and people; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they have
hearts which do not feel emotion, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
have eyes that do not see,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
have ears that do not hear.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">They
are like brute beasts, yet they have gone astray, they are the negligent
ones.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.180
Goddess has many excellent
names;<a href="#_ftn98" id="_ftnref98"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:
footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[98]</span></span></span></span></a>
therefore call on Her by the same;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
withdraw from those that use perverse names for Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">names
which do not reveal Her glory and magnificence; those that do this are
truly nonbelievers</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
their reward is nonexistent for such behavior.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.181 And
of those people that have been created,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">there
are certain people who can direct others with the truth and will act
justly according to our design.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.182 But
those that devise lies against our signs and miracles,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they will
fall gradually away from glory and happiness, and the method is one they
do not understand,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for it is
not punishment in the sense that people understand it,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
it is discipline and difficulties that direct them in the right
way.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.183
Such persons may live a long and prosperous life, but it will not be
happy or fulfilled,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
they do not have the guidance and counsel of heaven, and such a strategy
is most effective.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                     
</span> </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.184
They do not seem to understand that the prophetess has not taken any
devil for Her
companion,<a href="#_ftn99" id="_ftnref99"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:
footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[99]</span></span></span></span></a>
for the prophetesses are no more than public preachers and
teachers.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.185 But
some do not contemplate the Queendom of heaven and earth, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
things which Goddess has created;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
do not contemplate what will happen as their end draws near.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">What new
directions could they possibly find that are further away from the truth
of love </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
Goddess desires that they should know?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.186 For
if the hardness of a person’s heart causes them to err,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then she
has no true director, but unless one asks Her, She will leave them
wandering in confusion, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
each person has free will and She does not interfere with that.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                    
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.187
Many will inquire concerning the last hour of the last day, at what time
has it been fixed? </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But you
should answer them, the knowledge of this is only with the Lady of
Light; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">none
shall declare the fixed time, except Her.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The
expectation of this event will be a miracle unseen before in heaven and
on the earth, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but it is
not to be feared, for you have a loving Goddess. But it shall come upon
you all suddenly.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Many
people will ask you about this as if you were well informed of
this.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But you
should answer them that the knowledge of this event is with Goddess
alone,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
the vast majority of people will not know about it in advance.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                 
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.188 You
should tell the people, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">I myself
cannot obtain any advantage based upon what I do for myself, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor can I
avert any of the mischief I am to experience, this is the plan of
Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For if I
knew the secrets of Goddess for myself, I would certainly have an
abundance of good, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and evil
should never befall me, and I can tell you this has not happened, nor
will it ever.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Certainly
your prophetess is only an announcer of love and advice and
discipline,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
a messenger of good tidings to the people who will believe.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.189 It
is She who has created you each in pairs out of one soul for each
pair,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and on
this earth you may have a kindred soul who is your spouse, so you might
dwell with him.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And when
She created Eve, Eve carried a light burden for a time, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and she
walked easily, but as it became large and heavy, she called upon
Goddess, her Lady of Light, saying,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“If
You can give us this child without defects, we shall surely be
thankful.”<a href="#_ftn100" id="_ftnref100"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[100]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                   
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Yet when
She had given them a child without defects,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
began to worship the earthly idols of greed, power and self
centeredness,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and this
was despite the fact they had been given what they wanted: a child
without defects.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But far
be it from Goddess that they should have associated such negativity with
Her! </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.190 Eve
and Adam should have never associated these false, negative idols with
Goddess; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
negative idols create nothing because they are nothing.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                               
</span> </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.191
And these false negative idols can neither give them assistance, nor can
they help anyone.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.192 You
can invite them to the true direction, but many people,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">due to
the darkness and hardness of their own hearts will not follow you;
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">it
will be equal whether you invite them, or whether you hold your
peace.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                     
</span> </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.193
Certainly the false deities whom you invoke besides Goddess are like bad
servants to you.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                   </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.194 Try
such false negative idols, let them tempt you, and see if they give you
an answer </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which
brings you goodness and love.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                 
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.195 Do
such idols have feet to walk beside you?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Do they
have hands to caress you?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Do they
have eyes to look at you lovingly?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Do they
have ears to hear what you need in prayer?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Let the
others call upon these false idols to worship wealth and power; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
think they are laying a snare for others.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                      
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.196 For
Goddess is your protectress, who sent down the Book of the Korana and
Her love;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
She protects the righteous.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.197 If
you call upon false idols of wealth, greed and power, they cannot direct
you; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
cannot hear you.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                                         
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.198 You
see them looking enticing towards you, but they do not care about
you.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">You
can call them to guidance, but they will not hear you; they will look at
you but do not see you.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.199 Use
indulgence in alms, to the extent you can, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">command
what is just, and withdraw from the ignorant.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.200 If
an evil suggestion from a devil is sent to you, to divert you from your
duty,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">pray
to Goddess for assistance, for She hears and knows all.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.201
Certainly the people who love Goddess deeply, when a temptation from
Evil comes to them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they will
remember and be comforted by the divine commands,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
behold they can clearly see the danger of sin and error, and the wiles
of Evil.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.202 But
as for the darker entities themselves, they shall continue such actions
in error,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
afterwards they shall not be preserved from the detriments of their
actions.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.203 And
when you bring a verse of this Korana to them, they will say, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Did you
not just make this up yourself?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Answer,
“I follow only that which is revealed to me by My Lady of Light</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and all
Her good angels and spirits that surround Her. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The Book
itself contains evident proofs from your Lady of Light, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and it is
a direction and mercy to the believers.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.204 And
when the Korana is read, listen closely and keep silent; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
you can obtain all of its great mercies.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                        
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.205 And
meditate on your Lady of Light in your mind, with humility, love,
goodness and joy,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">without
loud speaking in the evening and morning; be not one of the
negligent.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">7.206
Moreover, the angels who are with my Lady of Light </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">do
not proudly disdain serving Her or loving Her, but they only celebrate
Her praise and worship Her.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">        
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:17.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;WP IconicSymbolsA&quot;">‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

class=Section13&gt;

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">BOOK
EIGHT<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>ENTITLED--THE SPOILS;
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">REVEALED
AT MEDINAH </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.1
People will ask you concerning spoils after battle;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Answer,
“The property which you have taken by force does not belong to you at
all, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and it
must be returned to the rightful owner or their legal heirs, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">recall
that you engaged in this battle as a matter of self defense, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and that
was your purpose, not to worship greed and
wealth.”<a href="#_ftn101" id="_ftnref101"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[101]</span></span></span></span></a>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Therefore
love Goddess and decide matters amicably amongst yourselves;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
obey Goddess and Her prophetesses, if you are indeed true
believers.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.2
Certainly the true believers are those whose hearts sing with hope and
love</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when the
word “Goddess” is mentioned, and whose faith increases </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when Her
signs and miracles are revealed to them, and those who trust in their
Lady of Light. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.3 They
are those who observe frequent prayer for themselves and their
families,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
for others, and who give alms out of the goodness of their hearts.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.4 These
are really the true believers; they shall have superior degrees of
happiness</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">with
their Lady of Light, and forgiveness, and honorable provisions.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.5 As
your Lady of Light brought you forth from Her house with truth;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
part of the believers were averse to the directions of their
prophetess,<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.6 they
disagreed with the prophetess concerning the truth, after it had been
made known to them, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which is
like a kind of death to their soul,<span style="mso-tab-count:1">     
</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which
always longs for the truth and love of Goddess as told by the
prophetesses.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                         
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.7 And
remember when Goddess promised you one of two parties for you to
evangelize,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that they
should be your new friends and assistants in the true religion,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
desired that one party was not furnished with provisions should be
delivered to you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.8 But
Goddess had a purpose to make known the truth in Her words,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and to
cut off the uttermost part of the unbelievers, that She might verify the
truth and destroy falsehood,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">although
the wicked ones were adverse thereto.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.9 When
you asked assistance of your Lady of Light and She answered you, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Certainly
I will assist you with a thousand angels, following one another in
order.”<a href="#_ftn102" id="_ftnref102"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:
footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[102]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                    </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.10 And
this Goddess designed only as a good tiding for you,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
your hearts might thereby rest secure;<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                         
</span> </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
victory is from Goddess alone, and Goddess is almighty and wise.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.11 When
a sleep fell on you as a security from Her,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
sent down upon you water from heaven, that She might thereby purify
you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and take
from you the abomination of evil, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
that She might confirm your hearts, and establish your feet
thereby.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.12 And
when the Lady of Light spoke to the angels, saying, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Certainly
I am with you; therefore confirm to me those that believe.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">I can
only cast longing hope into the hearts of the believers,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
their hearts are hard, knock at their heads, and poke the ends of their
fingers until they notice Me.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">         
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.13 This
they shall feel because they have resisted Goddess and Her
prophetesses,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">certainly
Goddess never angers, and does not punish, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
only loves and devises plans for those that act wrongfully.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                         
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.14 This
shall be what you would call discipline; you will be able to feel it and
taste it and know it;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
method utilized shall be like hell fire to wander in confusion</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">without
guidance and protection from Her, for those that will not believe.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.15 O
true believers, when you meet armed soldiers marching in great</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">numbers
against you, do not turn your backs when they are near,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for some
are treacherous and would be pleased to harm or kill you, yet still
invite them to peace.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But you
do not have to be like them, and you should always make peace and only
fight in self defense,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">as
necessary to protect life or property.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.16 For
if you turn your backs on them, unless you turn to dispute with
them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or
retreat to another part of the faithful, you may bring upon yourself a
danger that you did not anticipate,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">a
danger that may seem as if one were in hell, and it shall be a sad and
difficult journey!<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                 </span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.17 And
you did not evangelize those that died at Bedr yourselves,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
heaven allowed you to evangelize them by softening their hearts.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Nor did
you, O prophetess cast joy into their eyes, when you did seem to create
it, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
Goddess did this for you, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that She
might prove a miracle for the true believers by a gracious action from
Her,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
Goddess knows and sees everything.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.18 This
was also done that Goddess might also weaken the wiles</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">of
the unbelievers, because there were so many and you asked for Her
help.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                   
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.19 If
you desire a decision of matters between you and your opposition
now,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">a
decision has come to you, and if you desist from opposing the
prophetess, it will be better for you.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But if
you return to attack her sayings, heaven will return to assist
her;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and your
armed forces shall not be of advantage to you at all,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
though you are numerous and strong; for Goddess is with each of the
faithful,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
the pen and the tongue speaking words of love is much mightier than the
sword.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                                    
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.20 O
true believers, obey Goddess and Her prophetesses and do not turn away
from Her, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">since
you have already heard the good tidings of the Korana.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.21
And do not be as one of those that say, “We hear,” but they never
heard.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.22
Certainly, the worst sort of beasts in the sight of Goddess are the deaf
and the dumb to true religion,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">who
hear and understand nothing.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.23 If
Goddess had known any good in them, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She would
have certainly have caused them to hear accurately, and if She had
caused them to hear,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
would surely have turned back, and have left for places far away.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.24 O
true believers, answer Goddess and Her prophetess when She
invited</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you to
the table which gives you life,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and know
that Goddess is closest between a woman and her heart,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
that before Her you shall one day be assembled.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                        
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.25
Beware of sedition; it will not affect those among you that are
ungoddessly,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in
particular, but all of you in general; and know that Goddess is severe
in loving you.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                    </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.26 And
remember when you were few and reputed weak in the land,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
feared that women might snatch you away and kill you;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
Goddess provided you a place of refuge and She strengthened</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
with Her assistance, and She bestowed on you good things, that you might
give thanks to Her.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">               </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.27 O
true believers, do not deceive Goddess and Her prophetesses;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor
should you violate your faith against your own knowledge.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                      
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.28 And
know that your wealth and your children are a temptation in vanity to
you;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
that with Goddess is a great reward.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.29 O
true believers, if you love Goddess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She will
grant you a distinction and will expiate your sins from you,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
She will forgive you; for Goddess is endued with great liberality.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.30 And
remember when the unbelievers plotted against the prophetess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that they
might either detain the prophetess in bonds, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or put
her to death, or expel her from the city, and they plotted against her;
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
Goddess counteracted their evil plot, and Goddess is the best
Protectress.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.31 And
when heaven’s signs and miracles are repeated to some people, they
say,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“We have
heard; if we pleased we could have pronounced a composition</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">like
that for everyone, but this prophetess tells nothing but fables of the
ancients.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And when
they said, “O Goddess, if this is the truth from you, then rain down
stones upon us from heaven,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or
inflict upon us a grievous punishment.” <span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                        
</span><span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.32 But
Goddess is not disposed to punish anyone, for She does not punish or
harm,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor
was Goddess disposed to punish them when all they asked for was a
pardon.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.33 But
they have nothing to offer as an excuse for what nastiness they have
done, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">since
they have hindered the believers from visiting the holy temple, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">although
they are not the guardians thereof, only Goddess is,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
invites everyone to Her temples and houses of worship.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.34 The
guardians thereof are only those that love Goddess with</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">a
tenderness in their hearts, but the majority of people do not know
this.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                        
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.35 And
their prayer at the house of Goddess is nothing other than whistling and
clapping of the
hands.<a href="#_ftn103" id="_ftnref103"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[103]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Understand
therefore the difficulties that you have seen in the unbelievers.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                      
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.36 The
unbelievers only expend their wealth to obstruct the ways of
Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
perhaps they shall expend it, but afterwards it shall become a matter of
sighing, and of regret to them,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
at length they shall be overcome, and the unbelievers shall be gathered
together in one place<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.37 so
that Goddess may distinguish the wicked from the good, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
may throw the wicked together with one another, and may gather them in a
great crowd,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and lead
them into a place of cleansing and wholeness, but not until the final
resurrection.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">They
shall not perish, but shall be cleansed at the appointed time. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.38 Tell
the unbelievers that if they desist from opposing the
prophetesses,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">what is
already past shall be forgiven them, but if they return to attack her,
then the exemplary treatment</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">of
the former opposers of the prophetess is already past, and a similar
occurrence may happen to them.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.39
Therefore, fight non violently against the unbelievers until there is no
interest</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in
worshiping earthly idols of greed, wealth, self centeredness, war, hate
and aggression.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and treat
the prophetesses kindly and solicitously, and the religion shall be
completely given to Goddess.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">If
they desist, certainly Goddess sees all that they do.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                        
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.40 But
if they turn back again, know that Goddess is your patroness, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She
is the best patroness, and the best helper.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.41 And
know that whenever someone
<a href="#_ftn104" id="_ftnref104"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[104]</span></span></span></span></a>
gains any spoils by force or violence,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
spoils belong to the person or persons they were taken from,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or if
this cannot be determined, then to charity or the orphans,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
poor and the traveler in need, and this shall be done on the day that
the spoils were taken,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
shall be donated to a charity located where they were taken from;
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so
that you will have integrity in all that you do, for Goddess is
almighty.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                      
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
