mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.42 When
you were camped on the farthest side of the valley,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
another group was encamped on the other side, we created a caravan of
angels for you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
you might be protected and no harm would come to you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
your enemies always have an appointment with battles and war
mongering,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but you
were brought to evangelize the war mongers and bring peace to
them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
Goddess might accomplish Her objectives through peace and love;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
she who perishes hereafter might perish after seeing demonstrative
evidence,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and those
that lived might see the same evidence for Goddess both hears and knows
everything. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.43 When
your Lady of Light caused the enemy to appear to you in your dreams,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
were few in number, this was better, because if She caused them to
appear </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">numerous
to you, you would have been disheartened, thinking you could not
evangelize so many,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and then
you would dispute all of this with your prophetess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But
Goddess saves you from this, because She knows</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
understands the most intimate details of women.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.44 And
when She caused them to appear to you when you see them, to be few in
number in your eyes,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
appear to be few in number diminished in their eyes,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then
Goddess certainly accomplishes the matter which needed to be done.
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
to Goddess all things shall return.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.45 O
true believers, when you meet a party of unbelievers,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">stand
firm, and remember your Goddess frequently, that you might prosper.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                 
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.46 And
obey Goddess and Her prophetess, and do not hesitate,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">unless
you get discouraged, and your success departs from you;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
persevere with patience, for Goddess is with those that persevere.
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.47 And
do not be like some people who went out of their homes</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in an
insolent manner, with vain ostentation and arrogance toward other
women,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">who
were turned away from the ways of Goddess; for Goddess comprehends all
that they do.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                      </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.48 And
remember when Evil prepares work for them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and said
“No person shall prevail against you today; and I will certainly be near
to assist you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
may fight instead of evangelizing,” which is the opposite of what your
prophetess instructed you.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But when
the two opposing factions came near one another,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">evil
turned back on its heels, leaving many wounded, and said, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Certainly,
I am done with you, I can see things which you cannot see,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
you should love Goddess, for She is swift in loving you.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.49 When
the hypocrites, and those in whose hearts there was darkness said</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
their religion has deceived women; but whomever confides in
Goddess</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">can
never be deceived; for Goddess is mighty and wise.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                   
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.50 And
many saw when the unbelievers died at the hand of dark entities on
earth;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
struck their faces and their backs, and they said to them
cruelly,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Taste
the pain of burning; this you are suffering because of our hatred and
cruelty.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This is
how the dark entities behave; they are judgmental and hateful towards
each other.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But
Goddess is not; She is pure love.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.51 And
because Goddess is just towards Her servants, even those that do not
believe in Her, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She
felt their pain and had sympathy toward them.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.52 For
many had acted according to the designs of the people of Pharaoh,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and of
those before them, people who did not believe in the signs and miracles
of Goddess; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore
they were taken away in their darkness and wandering,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
they did not listen to the warning coming from the faithful as to
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">natural
disasters and the evil desires of other dark entities; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this
is because Goddess is mighty and severe in Her love for you all.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.53 This
has all come to pass because Goddess does not change Her grace,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">with
which She favors any people, until they change what is in their
hearts;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
for that, Goddess hears and sees all.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.54
According to the designs of the people of Pharaoh, and of those before
them, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">those
that charge the signs of their Lady of Light as being false;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">how
foolish have they acted; for they were destroyed because they did
not</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">listen to
the warnings and the prophetesses, they did not let go of their sin and
errors,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
accordingly they were drowned, those people of Pharaoh, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
were unjust persons and did not heed the signs.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                        
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.55
Certainly the worst cattle in the sight of Goddess are those that
are</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">obstinately
unfaithful, and they will not believe. They are the dark and grey
entities.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                       </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.56 As
to those who enter into an association with them,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
will violate trust in their friendships at every convenient
opportunity,<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.57 and
they do not love Goddess; if they are taken as hostage, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then
they are an example for those that come after them, and they are also a
warning.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                    </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.58 If
you apprehend treachery from any people, stay out of their league and
keep them from yours,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
Goddess does not care for the treacherous.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.59 And
do not think that the unbelievers have escaped Goddess’ knowledge,
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
they cannot weaken the power of Goddess, which is invincible.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                 
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.60
Therefore prepare against those that would spread oppression, hate,
cruelty and violence; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">work
against your enemies of darkness with whatever peaceable forces you are
able;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and have
troops of horses to distribute books and food and medicine,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and let
your vast supplies of food and wealth strike terror into your enemies,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that you
might solve famine, pestilence, and ignorance, so that your enemies,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which are
poor will not be able to control or influence any people on earth,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and this
applies to your enemies, and the enemies of Goddess, and people that you
might not know, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
Goddess knows them. And whatever you might expend in the defense of the
religion of Goddess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">it
shall be repaid to you, and you shall not be treated unjustly.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                         
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.61 And
if your neighbor inclines to keep the peace, then you should always
assist her to keep the peace,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
put you confidence in Goddess, because She sees and hears all.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.62 But
if they seek to deceive you, certainly Goddess will be your
support.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For
it is She who has strengthened you with Her help, and with that of the
unbeliever.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                    </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.63 And
She unites hearts in love. If you had expended whatever riches are in
the earth,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
could not unite the hearts of everyone, but Goddess can unite them, for
She is mighty and wise.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.64
Follow your prophetess, and Goddess shall be your support, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
such of the true believers who follow her.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                   
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.65 O
prophetess, stir up the faithful to any mission of aide and
assistance;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">if twenty
of you persevere with constancy, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
shall overcome two hundred wretched ones in need of help,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and if
there be one hundred of you, they shall overcome a thousand of those who
are in need of help, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
love is all that you need to understand. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.66 Now
Goddess has eased your minds, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for She
knows when you have been weakened by too much mission work, yet, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">if there
are a hundred of you that persevere with constancy during a mission of
assistance to the needy, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then you
shall overcome two hundred in need, and if there are a thousand of you,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then they
shall overcome with two thousand in need, by the permission of
Goddess;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
Goddess is with those who persevere.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.67 It
has not been granted that a prophetess should possess great
wealth,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">until she
has amassed many of the faithful on her side,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For you
seek the goods of this world, but Goddess regards highly </span>

class=Section14&gt;

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">only
the life to come; and Goddess is mighty and wise.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                    
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.68
Unless a revelation had been previously delivered from Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">certainly
difficulties and troubles have been part of your lives, as a
trial,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but the
people of Bedr will never forget how you came to their
assistance,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes"> </span>when they were poor and oppressed when
you were not much better off yourself.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                        </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.69 Eat
therefore of what you have acquired from your bounteous farms,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
which is healthy and good; for Goddess is gracious and merciful.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.70 O
prophetess, tell the needy that are in your hands,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">if
Goddess should know any good to be in your hearts, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She will
give you better than what you have given to them; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
She will forgive you your sins and errors, for Goddess is gracious and
merciful.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                         </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.71 But
if they seek to deceive you, then certainly they have deceived
Goddess;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
She has given the prophetess power over them; and Goddess is knowing and
wise.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.72
Moreover, those who have believed and fled their country,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
employed their wealth and person in assisting the religion of
Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and those
who have given the prophetess a refuge among them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and have
assisted her, these shall be deemed as next of kin to her.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But they
who have believed, but have not fled their country,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">shall
have no right of kindred until they also leave their country </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
become refugees for the sake of Goddess. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Yet if
they ask assistance of you on account of religion, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">it is up
to you to give them assistance, except as against a people between you
and yourselves </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">where
there is a treaty in existence; then you must adhere to that treaty, and
Goddess sees all that you do.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">    </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.73 And
as to the unbelievers, let them be deemed of relation one to the
other,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
should be considered as your neighbor to you, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
shall be kind toward them.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Unless
you do this, there will be increased unrest in the earth, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and more
meaningless battles will arise,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
much less love will come to you. Your goal is to increase the love in
the world, and not decrease it.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.74 But
as for those who have believed and left their country,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and have
done so for Goddess’ true religion, and who have given the prophetess
refuge among them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and have
assisted her, these are excellent believers; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
shall receive added mercy and an honorable provision.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">8.75 And
as for those who have believed since, and have fled their
country,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and who
have been with you, these are also counted as your kindred.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And those
who are related by blood shall be deemed the nearest of kin to one
another, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">preferably
to strangers, and all strangers are your neighbors.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This
is according to the good Book of Goddess; for Goddess knows all
things.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:17.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;WP IconicSymbolsA&quot;">‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes"> </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">BOOK NINE
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">ENTITLED
– THE DECLARATION OF IMMUNITY;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">REVEALED
AT MEDINA </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.1 This
is a declaration of immunity from Goddess and Her prophetess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">to those
that idolize wealth, greed and self centeredness,</span>

class=Section15&gt;

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">with
whom you have entered into an
agreement.<a href="#_ftn105" id="_ftnref105"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[105]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.2 Go to
and from in the earth securely for four months and prepare your works
better,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and know
that this does not weaken Goddess, and Goddess will show the unbelievers
Her path,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">as
a path of enlightenment and least resistance.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                  
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.3 And a
declaration of Scripture from Goddess and Her prophetess to the
people,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">on the
day of their pilgrimage, that not only is Goddess clear from the
negative actions of the unbelievers,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but also
She sends Her love and Scripture to Her
prophetess.<a href="#_ftn106" id="_ftnref106"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[106]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Accordingly
if you now repent, this would be better for you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but if
you turn back, know that you shall not weaken Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
instruct politely those that are unbelievers, for they will suffer to
wander the earth,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
they will have no protection from Goddess as the most difficult
discipline from Her.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                               </span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.4
Except such of the unbelievers which you have made an agreement</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for a
time certain, and who have not violated this agreement in any
manner,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor have
they assisted others in treachery against you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
should perform the agreement that you have made with them, until their
time shall have elapsed,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
Goddess loves those that keep their agreements.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                         
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.5 And
when the time has passed when you have granted them peace, then you
might further evangelize,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">wherever
you may find them, tell them what you will,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">besiege
them with your gospels politely, and wait for them with patience,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in every
convenient place try to talk to them regarding the peace and love of
your religion.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But if
they shall repent, and pray both morning and evening,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">give
to charity freely, love them greatly and have them as friends; for
Goddess is gracious and merciful.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.6 And
if any of the unbelievers shall pray for protection from you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then
grant them your protection, and tell them the good news that Goddess has
to offer; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
afterwards, help them reach a place of security. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This you
should do, because many people do not know the excellent religion
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
your prophetess has granted you.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.7 How
should the unbelievers be admitted into an association with Goddess
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and with
Her holy prophetess?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Except
places found in other ways, mostly at your house of worship. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">So long
as they behave with fidelity towards you, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
should also behave with fidelity towards them,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
Goddess loves all of Her people that love Her.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.8 How
can a person be admitted into an association with you?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">If they
prevail against you, they will not regard you as a relation or as a
person of their faith. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">They will
please you with what they say, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
their hearts may be averse to you, for many are wicked doers.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                   
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.9 This
is because they sell the signs of Goddess for a small price,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
they obstruct Her way; it is certainly dire mischief that they
practice.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                        
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.10 They
do not regard believers well, either in kindred or faith;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
hence they are in error and Goddess grieves for them.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.11 Yet
if they repent, and pray frequently or in morning and night,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and give
alms, they shall be deemed to be your true sister in religion.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Heaven
is pleased to show signs and a direction to people that desire to
understand this.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                </span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.12 But
if they violate their oaths, after joining your religion, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
perhaps even revile the religion, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">challenge
the leaders of the opposers to join you once again, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">(for
there might be no real trust in them at all), and they might desist from
treachery </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
quit earthly idols of wealth, power. greed and self centeredness and
love Goddess once again.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.13
Would you not challenge people who violate prior oaths,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when they
conspire to expel the prophetess of Goddess, yet they were against you
in the past?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Do you
not fear them? But it is more just that you should love Goddess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
put your faith in Her, if you are indeed a true believer.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.14 You
need not attack them, but instead show them the way,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
Goddess does not punish in the way you understand,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but She
will make plans for them, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
shall eventually arrive with you at the same place and time;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
will heal the hearts of those that believe; and cleanse the spirits of
the unpure. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.15 And
She will take away the indignation and arrogance</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in
their hearts, for Goddess turns to all that ask for Her; and Goddess is
knowing and wise.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                            </span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.16 Have
you ever thought that you were abandoned by Goddess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
there were few in alliance with you?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Have you
felt as though you were the only one among you that understood Her true
and loving religion?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Or,
perhaps you were the only one that understood Goddess and Her
prophetess, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
you only had the faithful for a few friends?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.17 It
is not fitting that the unbelievers should just visit the temple,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when they
still have disbelief in their hearts because they have been war
mongering,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
have not shown them the way; allow them to visit, but show them your
religion, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
kindness of your hearts, and your love for Goddess in glowing smiles as
they come to you.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.18 Of
course, the best person to visit the temples of Goddess</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">are those
that believe in Goddess and the last day, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and are
faithful to prayer in the morning and evening,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">gives
alms freely and not of a dictate, and who loves Goddess greatly</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
should not put undue restrictions upon them to visit;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">such
as permission from others, or that they believe in a certain way foreign
to your understanding.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.19
Understand that the giving of food and drink to the pilgrims,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
visiting of your local temple are just as meritorious</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">as those
acts performed by people who believe in Goddess</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
last day and they love the religion of Goddess. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">All kind
people are held equal in the eyes of Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">all acts
of love, kindness and compassion are held equal in the eyes of
Goddess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
Goddess directs the righteous , kind and loving people.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.20 For
the people who have believed and fled their country,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
employed their resources and their persons out of their love for the
religion of Goddess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">shall
be held in great degree of honor with Goddess, and these people shall be
very happy.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.21 The
Lady of Light sends good tidings of mercy from Her,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
goodwill, and the believers shall have gardens wherein they shall enjoy
lasting pleasure;<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                         
</span> </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.22
further they shall continue therein forever; for with Goddess is a great
reward.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                        </span>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.23 O
true believers, take not your parents or siblings as true
friends,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">if they
love infidelity, war, hate, aggression and rage above faith; yet be
respectful to them;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet
note many are likely to be unjust doers, so protect yourselves.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                   
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.24 If
your mothers, and your daughters, and your sisters and your
husbands,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and your
relations, and your substance which you have acquired,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and your
merchandise which you fear should not be sold off</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">are more
dear to you than Goddess, and Her prophetess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
advancement of a kind and loving religion, wait until Goddess shall send
Her command,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
Goddess does not direct the unbeliever.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.25
Goddess has now assisted you in many engagements and travails,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
particularly at
Honein<a href="#_ftn107" id="_ftnref107"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[107]</span></span></span></span></a>,
where there were many in the multitudes to convert others, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but there
was no actual manner of advantage to you, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the earth
was not sufficiently straight for you to
escape,<a href="#_ftn108" id="_ftnref108"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[108]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
forgot that it was indeed spacious, yet you abandoned this test
and</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
turned your backs on those that you were there to preach to.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                    
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.26
Afterwards Goddess sent down Her troops of
angels<a href="#_ftn109" id="_ftnref109"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[109]</span></span></span></span></a>
which you did not see;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
took no heed of those that were not steadfast in belief;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and this
was the reward of the unbelievers, to wander in confusion.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.27 And
Goddess will turn in mercy to those whom She loves, who have first loved
Her,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
She is the Most Forgiving and Most Merciful one.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.28 O
true believers, notice that many of the idolaters of wealth, greed,
power and self centeredness </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">are
unclean, that is, dishonest in their work and habits;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore,
you must show them the way and invite them to your
temple,<a href="#_ftn110" id="_ftnref110"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[110]</span></span></span></span></a>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
especially after this year, and as you are able. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And if
you find you need anything because the unbelievers have cut off trade
and communication, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
will enrich you, of Her abundance, for Goddess is knowing and
wise.<a href="#_ftn111" id="_ftnref111"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[111]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.29
Oppose those who do not believe in Goddess and the last day </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when they
do something evil or unjust, and forbid not what Goddess or Her
prophetess has not forbidden, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
profess the true religion unto those whom the Scriptures have been
delivered, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
they should not be required to pay any tribute to you for
this.<a href="#_ftn112" id="_ftnref112"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[112]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.30 The
Jews say Ezra is the Child of Goddess, and the Christians say that
Yeshua is the Child of Goddess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This is
what they say, for we are all Children of Goddess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
they are repeating Scriptures written long ago; </span>

class=Section16&gt;

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">may
Goddess love them for their
faithfulness!<a href="#_ftn113" id="_ftnref113"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[113]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.31 They
know that many priestesses and nuns have been prophetesses,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">out of
their love for their Goddess, as well as Yeshua, the child of Mother
Mary; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for they
have been commanded to worship One True Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">there is
no Goddess but She; and any name you call Her by, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
those names of male deities, which are so numerous,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">are
still nothing but one, in the One True Goddess.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.32 They
seek to illuminate the light of Goddess with their mouths,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
Goddess needs many to spread Her light, although the infidels will be
adverse to this.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                             </span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.33 It
is She who has sent Her prophetess with the direction and true
religion;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that She
may cause it to appear superior to every other religion, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">although
the idolaters are adverse to this.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.34 O
true believers, certainly many of the priestesses and nuns take the
resources of their people </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for good
use by the church; and in doing so they show their love for
Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But for
those people who treasure up gold and silver, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
employ none of it for the advancement of Goddess’ true religion, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
will suffer wandering and confusion on earth.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.35 On
the day of judgment their treasures will be shown to them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and their
foreheads, sides and backs shall be filled with grief,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
angels will say, “look at what you have treasured up,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">now see
the suffering of the people that lived near you that they could have
helped,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">now see
how their lives could have been so much better.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And they
will taste and feel the poverty and hunger they created, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which
is proper discipline for their understanding.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.36
Moreover, the complete number of months with Goddess is twelve
months,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which
were ordained in the Book of Goddess on the day</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">where She
created the heavens and the earth, of these, four are more
sacred.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This is
the right religion; it is for people who are correctly directed,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore
be assiduous in dealing righteously and ready with forgiveness in these
months.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But
preach to the idolaters of wealth, greed and power, in all the months
you see them,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
know that Goddess is with those that love
Her.<a href="#_ftn114" id="_ftnref114"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[114]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                      
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.37 Many
have been led into error by this, they allow a month to be violated one
year,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then
declare it sacred another year, now you might all agree in the number of
months </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
Goddess has directed you to keep sacred; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
some have incorrectly proclaimed that Goddess has forbidden this when
She has not.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                </span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.38 The
problems with the actions of some believers have been noted and
corrected; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
does not direct the unbelievers unless and until they call upon Her to
do so. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Rest
assured that the reward of the present life is</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">negligible
when compared with the life which is yet to come.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                          
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.39
Unless you help the poor and the homeless when you are summoned to them,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you will
be greatly disappointed on the day of your resurrection when you see and
feel</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">how they
had suffered and how you could have helped this suffering,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet
Goddess does not suffer by this; She will send another helper in your
stead,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
another and another, until those that prayed to Her in need have been
properly helped; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
shall have not hurt Her at all; for Goddess is almighty,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but when
you refuse to assist a needy person when requested, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
only forego yet another opportunity to improve your own soul.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.40 If
you do not assist your prophetess, still Goddess will find others to
assist her,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">as She
assisted her before when the prophetess was driven out of Mecca,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
second of two; first when she was in the cave; then when she said to her
friends, during difficult times,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Do not
be grieved, for Goddess is with us.” </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
Goddess sent Her
peace<a href="#_ftn115" id="_ftnref115"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[115]</span></span></span></span></a>
down upon the prophetess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
strengthened her with armies of angels, but you did not see this.
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And She
made the world of those that believed to not be abased,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
the word of Goddess was exalted; for Goddess is almighty and wise.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.41 Go
forth and assist Goddess and the prophetess </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in their
work for peace and love and harmony throughout the world,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
employ your substance and your person for the advancement of Goddess’
religion.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This
is always better for you, if only you knew it.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.42 If
there was much advantage in the way and a moderate journey,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
prophetess would readily been followed; but the way was difficult and
tedious,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet they
swear by Goddess, saying “If we had been able, we would have gone with
you.” </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But
they fail to enhance their souls with such an attitude, for Goddess sees
how strong they actually are.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">       
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.43 May
Goddess forgive them all for what they do! </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Many
stayed at home and made excuses for themselves, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
Goddess knew what they were doing when they stayed at home.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                              
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.44 Many
of the people who believe in Goddess and the last day </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">will not
ask to be excused from helping Goddess with their substance and their
person </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for the
advancement of Goddess’ religion; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet
all would have helped if they knew how much Goddess loves them.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                         
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.45
Certainly most that only want to be excused from helping Goddess</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">do not
truly believe in Goddess and the day of their resurrection, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
have doubts concerning faith;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">wherefore
they toss themselves back and forth in their doubting.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                     
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.46 If
they had been willing to go and assist the prophetess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they had
certainly prepared for that purpose a provision of food and medical
supplies to help others,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
Goddess knew they were adverse to going out to help others,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
are most slothful, and it was said to them, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Perhaps
you should stay behind with others that are resolved to stay
behind.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.47 If
they had gone with the prophetess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
would have only have been a burden to her,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
would have run about and stirred others to mischief and sedition and
there would have been</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">some
among them that would have listened, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
Goddess knows those that do not have the prerequisite good
intentions.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                 
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.48 Some
people formerly sought to engage in sedition, and they disturbed the
affairs of the prophetess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">until the
truth came out, and the decree of Goddess was made obvious,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">despite
the fact that they were adverse to this.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                   
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.49 The
are some people who have said to the prophetess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">please
allow me to stay behind, and do not expose me to temptation,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but then
have they not fallen to temptation already at
home?<a href="#_ftn116" id="_ftnref116"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[116]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But
love will certainly embrace all and Goddess will show them the right
path.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.50 If
good happens to the prophetess, it grieves many unbelievers;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but if a
misfortune befalls her, they say, “We knew we should stay at home
because this would happen,”</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
they turn their backs and rejoice at the mishap.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                           
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.51 But
you should say, “Nothing will befall the faithful, except what Goddess
has decreed for us; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She
is our patroness and only the faithful put their trust in Goddess.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                               
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.52 Tell
the people, “Do you expect any other mishap should befall us,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">other
than two wonderful things; either victory or martyrdom? </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But we
expect that no matter what happens,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
loves all Her people and She will make plans for those that are not on
the right path.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Wait
therefore to see what will happen over time, and we will patiently wait
for you to see this.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.53 Tell
the people, “Expend your money in pious uses, either voluntarily or by
constraint,”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and even
the most wicked can oftentimes be encouraged to do something good and
kind for another,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
no good deed is ever overlooked by Goddess, and She rejoices in them
all.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                             
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.54 Tell
the people, nothing hinders their contributions from being accepted and
put to good use,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">whether
or not that person yet believes in Goddess and Her prophetesses,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
those that do not pray, even those that pray sluggishly,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
even those that expend their resources for the service of Goddess on a
basis that is fairly unwilling. Nothing is overlooked by Goddess.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                                    
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.55 Let
not riches or children cause you to marvel at another person.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Certainly
Goddess only intends to test them in the world,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
perhaps their souls may depart this world while they are unbelievers,
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
this should be of no concern to you.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                            
</span> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">9.56 Many
